דָּא

דאג

to fear, to worry, to be anxious, to be afraid, to be distressed \= state in which humans experience fear, anxiety, or distress ◄ out of uncertainty of what might happen to themselves or their beloved ones; ► which may express itself in trembling and shaking of the body

## דאה (id: 001538000000000)

דאה
===

דאה (H1675)

verb · דָּאָה · דַּיָּה

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ עוף

to swoop down \= action by which a bird moves swiftly downwards ► in order to capture its prey; ≈ often used metaphorically to refer to an army attacking the enemy

[DEU 28:49](https://ref.ly/Deut28:49) · [PSA 18:11](https://ref.ly/Ps18:11) · [JER 48:40](https://ref.ly/Jer48:40) · [JER 49:22](https://ref.ly/Jer49:22)

1 DEU 33:2 RSV NJPS GNT \| MT\-K אשׁדת \| MT\-Q אֵשׁ דָּת "fiery law" \| NIV "mountain slopes" \= אֲשֵׁדָה

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 28:49; Psalms 18:11; Jeremiah 48:40; Jeremiah 49:22


## דָּאָה (id: 001539000000000)

דָּאָה
======

דָּאָה (H1676)

noun f · דאה

Birds 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ רָאָה

black kite \= bird of prey, dark brown with a greyish head and a long V\-shaped tail, flies relatively low and slowly; feeds on insects, frogs, lizards, and food scraps from human dwellings, and scavenges dead fish or other dead animals; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:14](https://ref.ly/Lev11:14)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:14


## דֹּב (id: 001540000000000)

דֹּב
====

דֹּב (H1677 · A1678)

noun

Wild Animals

(Syrian brown) bear \= large mammal with thick fur and a rather doglike face; walks on all fours but may stand up on its back legs to get a better view; maybe 2 meters tall when standing up and weigh over 200 kilos; feeds on roots, berries, wild fruit, mice, and lizards, and, occasionally, small livestock; ◄ \|iUrsus arctos syriacus\|i\*; ► dangerous when provoked or robbed of cubs; ≈ associated with violence and danger

[1SA 17:34](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:34) · [1SA 17:36](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:36) · [1SA 17:37](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:37) · [2SA 17:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:8) · [2KI 2:24](https://ref.ly/2Kgs2:24) · [PRO 17:12](https://ref.ly/Prov17:12) · [PRO 28:15](https://ref.ly/Prov28:15) · [ISA 11:7](https://ref.ly/Isa11:7) · [ISA 59:11](https://ref.ly/Isa59:11) · [LAM 3:10](https://ref.ly/Lam3:10) · [DAN 7:5](https://ref.ly/Dan7:5) · [HOS 13:8](https://ref.ly/Hos13:8) · [AMO 5:19](https://ref.ly/Amos5:19)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 17:34; 1 Samuel 17:36; 1 Samuel 17:37; 2 Samuel 17:8; 2 Kings 2:24; Proverbs 17:12; Proverbs 28:15; Isaiah 11:7; Isaiah 59:11; Lamentations 3:10; Daniel 7:5; Hosea 13:8; Amos 5:19

## דִּבָּה (id: 001543000000000)

דִּבָּה
=======

דִּבָּה (H1681)

noun f

Speak

bad report, slander, gossip \= action by which humans give a verbal report concerning circumstances or events, usually with evil intentions

[GEN 37:2](https://ref.ly/Gen37:2) · [NUM 13:32](https://ref.ly/Num13:32) · [NUM 14:36](https://ref.ly/Num14:36) · [NUM 14:37](https://ref.ly/Num14:37) · [PSA 31:14](https://ref.ly/Ps31:14) · [PRO 10:18](https://ref.ly/Prov10:18) · [PRO 25:10](https://ref.ly/Prov25:10) · [JER 20:10](https://ref.ly/Jer20:10)

Objects

object of gossip literally: gossip; hence: \= an object that is talked about by others, usually with evil intentions

[EZK 36:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:3)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 37:2; Numbers 13:32; Numbers 14:36; Numbers 14:37; Psalms 31:14; Proverbs 10:18; Proverbs 25:10; Jeremiah 20:10; Ezekiel 36:3


## דְּבֹורָה (id: 001544000000000)

דְּבֹורָה
=========

דְּבֹורָה (H1682 · H1683)

noun f · דבר

Swarming Creatures 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ זְבוּב

bee \= flying insect that collects nectar from flowers and converts it into honey; lives in swarms made up of many thousands of insects; stings only when threatened; ≈ with connotations ranging from positive (food producing) to negative (as a metaphor for an army of well\-organized enemies

[DEU 1:44](https://ref.ly/Deut1:44) · [JDG 14:8](https://ref.ly/Judg14:8) · [PSA 118:12](https://ref.ly/Ps118:12) · [ISA 7:18](https://ref.ly/Isa7:18)

name · דבר

Names of People

Deborah \= woman; ► nurse of Rebekah

[GEN 35:8](https://ref.ly/Gen35:8)

Names of People

Deborah \= woman; ► wife of Lappidoth; prophetess, warrior and judge of Israel in the pre\-monarchical period

[JDG 4:4](https://ref.ly/Judg4:4) · [JDG 4:5](https://ref.ly/Judg4:5) · [JDG 4:9](https://ref.ly/Judg4:9) · [JDG 4:10](https://ref.ly/Judg4:10) · [JDG 4:14](https://ref.ly/Judg4:14) · [JDG 5:1](https://ref.ly/Judg5:1) · [JDG 5:7](https://ref.ly/Judg5:7) · [JDG 5:12](https://ref.ly/Judg5:12) · [JDG 5:15](https://ref.ly/Judg5:15)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 1:44; Judges 14:8; Psalms 118:12; Isaiah 7:18; Genesis 35:8; Judges 4:4; Judges 4:5; Judges 4:9; Judges 4:10; Judges 4:14; Judges 5:1; Judges 5:7; Judges 5:12; Judges 5:15


## דבח (id: 001545000000000)

דבח
===

דבח (A1684)

verb

Sacrifice 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pe'al

to sacrifice \= the human activity of killing one or more animals as a religious sacrifice; usually part of the animal is offered to the deity and part is eaten by the worshipers; often accompanied by the burning of incense

[EZR 6:3](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:3)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Ezra 6:3

## דבק (id: 001552000000000)

דבק
===

דבק (H1692 · A1693)

verb · דָּבֵק · דֶּבֶק

Attach 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pu'al, verb qal, verb pe'al 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ יצק

to stick together, to cling together \= state in which objects are closely compacted together

[JOB 38:38](https://ref.ly/Job38:38) · [JOB 41:9](https://ref.ly/Job41:9) · [JOB 41:15](https://ref.ly/Job41:15) · [DAN 2:43](https://ref.ly/Dan2:43)

Attach 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hof

to cling, to cleave, to stick, to freeze \= state in which an object is positioned around or against another object in such a way that the two cannot be separated easily

[DEU 13:18](https://ref.ly/Deut13:18) · [2SA 23:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:10) · [JOB 19:20](https://ref.ly/Job19:20) · [JOB 29:10](https://ref.ly/Job29:10) · [JOB 31:7](https://ref.ly/Job31:7) · [PSA 22:16](https://ref.ly/Ps22:16) · [PSA 44:26](https://ref.ly/Ps44:26) · [PSA 102:6](https://ref.ly/Ps102:6) · [PSA 119:25](https://ref.ly/Ps119:25) · [PSA 137:6](https://ref.ly/Ps137:6) · [JER 13:11](https://ref.ly/Jer13:11) · [LAM 4:4](https://ref.ly/Lam4:4)

Attach 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to cause to cling, to cause to cleave, to cause to stick \= causative action by which someone causes something else to be positioned around or against another object in such a way that the two cannot be separated easily

[EZK 3:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:26) · [EZK 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:4) · [EZK 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:4)

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to cling, to cleave, to overtake literally: to cling to someone; hence: \= to happen to someone ◄ as if the event has physically attached itself to the one undergoing it; ≈ only used for negative events

[GEN 19:19](https://ref.ly/Gen19:19) · [DEU 28:60](https://ref.ly/Deut28:60) · [2KI 5:27](https://ref.ly/2Kgs5:27) · [JER 42:16](https://ref.ly/Jer42:16)

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to cause to cling, to cause to cleave to, to cause to overtake literally: to cause to cling to someone; hence: \= causative action by which someone causes something to happen to someone else ◄ as if the event has been physically attached to the one undergoing it; ≈ only used for negative events

[DEU 28:21](https://ref.ly/Deut28:21)

Associate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to cling, to stay, to commit oneself \= action by which someone commits oneself to remain closely involved with another person or group, out of affection and/or solidarity

[GEN 2:24](https://ref.ly/Gen2:24) · [GEN 34:3](https://ref.ly/Gen34:3) · [NUM 36:7](https://ref.ly/Num36:7) · [NUM 36:9](https://ref.ly/Num36:9) · [DEU 10:20](https://ref.ly/Deut10:20) · [DEU 11:22](https://ref.ly/Deut11:22) · [DEU 13:5](https://ref.ly/Deut13:5) · [DEU 30:20](https://ref.ly/Deut30:20) · [JOS 22:5](https://ref.ly/Josh22:5) · [JOS 23:8](https://ref.ly/Josh23:8) · [JOS 23:12](https://ref.ly/Josh23:12) · [RUT 1:14](https://ref.ly/Ruth1:14) · [RUT 2:8](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:8) · [RUT 2:21](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:21) · [RUT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:23) · [2SA 20:2](https://ref.ly/2Sam20:2) · [1KI 11:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:2) · [2KI 3:3](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:3) · [2KI 18:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:6) · [PSA 63:9](https://ref.ly/Ps63:9) · [PSA 101:3](https://ref.ly/Ps101:3) · [PSA 119:31](https://ref.ly/Ps119:31)

Associate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to cause to cling, to cause to commit oneself \= causative action by which someone causes someone else to commit oneself to remain closely involved with another person or group, out of affection and/or solidarity

[JER 13:11](https://ref.ly/Jer13:11)

Pursue 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ יּשׂג

to be in close pursuit, to catch up \= action by which someone pursues another person or group closely enough to be able to inflict harm

[GEN 31:23](https://ref.ly/Gen31:23) · [JDG 18:22](https://ref.ly/Judg18:22) · [JDG 20:45](https://ref.ly/Judg20:45) · [1SA 14:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:22) · [1SA 31:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam31:2) · [2SA 1:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam1:6) · [1CH 10:2](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:2)

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to catch up literally: to catch up with someone; hence: \= process by which something happens to someone else ◄ as if the event had been pursuing the one undergoing it and was finally able to catch up; ≈ only used for negative events

[JDG 20:42](https://ref.ly/Judg20:42)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Job 38:38; Job 41:9; Job 41:15; Daniel 2:43; Deuteronomy 13:18; 2 Samuel 23:10; Job 19:20; Job 29:10; Job 31:7; Psalms 22:16; Psalms 44:26; Psalms 102:6; Psalms 119:25; Psalms 137:6; Jeremiah 13:11; Lamentations 4:4; Ezekiel 3:26; Ezekiel 29:4; Genesis 19:19; Deuteronomy 28:60; 2 Kings 5:27; Jeremiah 42:16; Deuteronomy 28:21; Genesis 2:24; Genesis 34:3; Numbers 36:7; Numbers 36:9; Deuteronomy 10:20; Deuteronomy 11:22; Deuteronomy 13:5; Deuteronomy 30:20; Joshua 22:5; Joshua 23:8; Joshua 23:12; Ruth 1:14; Ruth 2:8; Ruth 2:21; Ruth 2:23; 2 Samuel 20:2; 1 Kings 11:2; 2 Kings 3:3; 2 Kings 18:6; Psalms 63:9; Psalms 101:3; Psalms 119:31; Genesis 31:23; Judges 18:22; Judges 20:45; 1 Samuel 14:22; 1 Samuel 31:2; 2 Samuel 1:6; 1 Chronicles 10:2; Judges 20:42


## דֶּבֶק (id: 001553000000000)

דֶּבֶק
======

דֶּבֶק (H1694)

noun m · דבק

Attach

fastening, soldering \= area where two objects have been joined together permanently

[ISA 41:7](https://ref.ly/Isa41:7)

Attach 

|  |
| --- |

 Clothing 

|  |
| --- |

 Weapons

joint, plate \= object that joins different parts to make them one whole

[1KI 22:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:34) · [2CH 18:33](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:33)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 41:7; 1 Kings 22:34; 2 Chronicles 18:33


## דָּבֵק (id: 001554000000000)

דָּבֵק
======

דָּבֵק (H1695)

adj

Attach

joined to, touching \= state of being positioned against another object in such a way that the two cannot be separated easily

[2CH 3:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr3:12)

Associate

commited, devoted \= state in which someone is closely involved with another person or deity, out of affection and/or solidarity

[DEU 4:4](https://ref.ly/Deut4:4) · [PRO 18:24](https://ref.ly/Prov18:24)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Chronicles 3:12; Deuteronomy 4:4; Proverbs 18:24


## דבר (id: 001555000000000)

דבר
===

דבר (H1696)

verb · דֶּבֶר

Non\-Exist 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to destroy, to get rid of, to do away with \= causative action by which someone exterminates a group of people, either directly or by the hands of someone else

[2CH 22:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:10)1

Control 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to subdue \= action or process by which a nation gains control over someone else, usually involving violence

[PSA 18:48](https://ref.ly/Ps18:48) · [PSA 47:4](https://ref.ly/Ps47:4)

verb · דָּבָר · דִּבֵּר · דִּבְרָה · דַּבְּרָה · דִּבְרִי

Speak 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pi, verb pu'al 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אמר · הגה · חבר בְּמִלִּים · נבא · נגד · ספר · עוד · צוה · קרא

to speak, to mention, to tell \= action by which humans and deities utter words; this can happen within their minds and be inaudible to others, but in most cases the words are spoken out loud in order to communicate something to others; usually not directly followed by the actual words that are spoken

Speak 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to speak together \= action by which groups of humans utter words in order to communicate something among themselves

[PSA 119:23](https://ref.ly/Ps119:23) · [EZK 33:30](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:30) · [MAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Mal3:13) · [MAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Mal3:16)

1 2CH 22:10 DCH "drive out, pursue" 2 1SA 25:39 Exact meaning unsure. 3 1KI 12:7 MT\-K וידבר \| MT\-Q וַיְדַבְּרוּ 4 JOB 19:18 RSV NRSV ESV "talk against me" NIV "ridicule me" NJPS "speak against me" NJB " start jeering at me" GNT "laugh" CEV "make fun" Craigie "jeer at" Pope "revile" \| REB "turn their backs on me" DCH Clines "turn the back" 5 PSA 127:5 RSV NRSV ESV "speaks with" NIV NJPS "contend with" NJB "in dispute with" REB "confronted by" GNT "meets with" CEV "attack with arguments" Allen "argue" \| DCH Dahood "to drive out" 6 PRO 21:28 RSV ESV "word will endure" NJPS NRSV "testify" NJB "not be silenced" REB "speak on" \| GNT "word is accepted" Allen "speaks" Bruce "testify" Fox "speak" \| DCH "destroy" NIV "be destroyed" 7 SNG 5:6 RSV NRSV CEV ESV "spoke" NJPS "said" \| DCH "turn the back" NIV "departure" NJB "flight" REB "turned his back" 8 ISA 58:13 RSV "talking idly" NIV "speaking idle words" \| DCH "manage" NRSV "pursuing your own affairs" REB "attending to your own affairs" \| NJPS "strike bargains" 9 JER 3:5 MT\-K דברתי \| MT\-Q דִבַּרְתְּ 10 JER 23:17 MT HOTTP\-C NIV NJPS NJB \| RSV NRSV REB GNT ESV "the word" \= דָּבָר

## דִּבֵּר (id: 001556000000000)

דִּבֵּר
=======

דִּבֵּר (H1699b)

noun m · דבר

Speak

speech, word, one who speaks exact meaning uncertain; either: \= the act of speaking; or: \= something that is spoken; or: \= the faculty or power to speak; or: \= one who speaks

[JER 5:13](https://ref.ly/Jer5:13)1

1 JER 5:13 RSV NIV NJB NRSV REB "word" \| NJPS "Word"

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 5:13


## דֶּבֶר (id: 001557000000000)

דֶּבֶר
======

דֶּבֶר (H1698)

noun m · דבר

Weak 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ רָעָה · קֶּטֶב

pestilence, plague in a strict sense: \= an epidemic disease ► that causes high mortality; in a wider sense: \= any widespread affliction, calamity, or evil, ≈ especially one regarded as a direct punishment by God

words, message \= words spoken by humans and deities and, in certain cases, written down

Speak 

|  |
| --- |

 noun m sg

word, words, message literally: word; hence: \= a collection of words spoken by humans and deities and, in certain cases, written down

## דֹּבֶר (id: 001559000000000)

דֹּבֶר
======

דֹּבֶר (H1699a)

noun m · דבר

Land

pasture, meadow \= open land with enough grass and plants to graze cattle or flocks of sheep and goats

[ISA 5:17](https://ref.ly/Isa5:17) · [MIC 2:12](https://ref.ly/Mic2:12)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 5:17; Micah 2:12


## דִּבְרָה (id: 001560000000000)

דִּבְרָה
========

דִּבְרָה (H1700 · A1701)

noun f · דבר

Conflict

case, cause \= an action or suit at law, as well as the evidence offered to support its claims

[JOB 5:8](https://ref.ly/Job5:8)

Description

manner, pattern exact meaning unsure; possibly: \= a certain role or pattern of behavior

[PSA 110:4](https://ref.ly/Ps110:4)1

Perception

**Collocation:** עַד דִּבְרַת · עַל דִּבְרַת

the cause of, with regard to, because of, in order that \= particle linking two propositions, denoting a causal relation between the two

[ECC 3:18](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:18) · [ECC 7:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:14) · [ECC 8:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:2) · [DAN 2:30](https://ref.ly/Dan2:30) · [DAN 4:14](https://ref.ly/Dan4:14)

1 PSA 110:4 Most English versions have "the order of", implying some (priestly) class or rank. But the word is probably to be understood here in a modal sense (cf. Allen, Psalms 100–150, p.79–82\) \| NJPS has a different understanding: "a rightful king by My decree", understanding the word as meaning an official communication.

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Job 5:8; Psalms 110:4; Ecclesiastes 3:18; Ecclesiastes 7:14; Ecclesiastes 8:2; Daniel 2:30; Daniel 4:14

## דגל (id: 001571000000000)

דגל
===

דגל (H1713)

verb · דֶּגֶל

Arrange 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to array oneself with banners \= action by which a group divides itself into smaller groups, organized with the help of banners

[PSA 20:6](https://ref.ly/Ps20:6)1

Soldiers 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

army with banners \= group of soldiers wielding banners; ≈ considered a beautiful, though frightening, sight

[SNG 6:4](https://ref.ly/Song6:4)2 · [SNG 6:10](https://ref.ly/Song6:10)2

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to be prominent, to stand out \= to possess more of a certain quality than one's peers and therefore stand out among them; ◄ compared to a banner, which, when one looks at an army, is prominently visible

[SNG 5:10](https://ref.ly/Song5:10)

1 PSA 20:6 DCH suggests a possible alternative, "wait upon", from a proposed root דגל II, "look, wait upon" 2 SNG 6:4 · SNG 6:10 Most versions and scholars interpret נִּדְגָּלֹות as deriving from דֶגֶל "banner". Another possibility takes דגל as meaning "look' (HALOT \| DCH) and the pt. pass. as "sight"; the arguments are well presented by Gerleman, Ruth/Hohelied, p. 182–83 (cf. also Zakovitch, Das Hohelied, p.232–33\). If נִּדְגָּלֹות is taken as pointing to the stars (REB CEV), than the meaning here would be "majestic as the stars". In this case, the lexical domain would be "Universe \> Intense", and the contextual domain "Beauty \| Nature \> Human".

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 20:6; Song of Songs 6:4; Song of Songs 6:10; Song of Songs 5:10

## דגר (id: 001574000000000)

דגר
===

דגר (H1716)

verb

Cover 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ בקע

to hatch \= to sit upon eggs for a prolonged period ► in order to provide the warmth that is needed for the eggs to hatch at the proper time

[ISA 34:15](https://ref.ly/Isa34:15)1 · [JER 17:11](https://ref.ly/Jer17:11)

1 ISA 34:15 The exact meaning of דגר here is much discussed. There is a succession of 3 verbs indicating actions of a mother\-bird in relation to eggs. NRSV translates בקע as "hatch" and דגר as "brood", and NJPS the other way round, though interpreting them as practically synonyms \| RSV REB "gather", implying a movement that either comes before the hatching or (in some way) after it, as the order in the text suggests. The best course could be to follow the meaning of דגר in JER 17:11, which with more probability points to "hatch".

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 34:15; Jeremiah 17:11

## דהם (id: 001583000000000)

דהם
===

דהם (H1724)

verb

Unable 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to be stunned, to be astonished, to be taken by surprise \= state in which humans are unable to act, ◄ as a physical and mental reaction to some news or event

[JER 14:9](https://ref.ly/Jer14:9)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 14:9


## דהר (id: 001584000000000)

דהר
===

דהר (H1725)

verb · דַּהֲרָה

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ מֵרְכָּבָה מְרַקֵּדָה

to gallop \= action by which a horse walks at a fast pace, with all the feet off the ground together in each stride

[NAM 3:2](https://ref.ly/Nah3:2)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Nahum 3:2


## דַּהֲרָה (id: 001585000000000)

דַּהֲרָה (H1726)

noun f · דהר

Move

galloping \= action by which a horse walks at a fast pace, with all the feet off the ground together in each stride

## דֹּואֵג (id: 001586000000000)

דֹּואֵג
=======

דֹּואֵג (H1673) — דֹּאֵג

name

Names of People

Doeg \= man; ◄ Edomite; ► official, during the time of king Saul, who betrayed the whereabouts of David to his master and later killed the priests of YHWH

[1SA 21:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam21:8) · [1SA 22:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:9) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [1SA 22:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:22) · [PSA 52:2](https://ref.ly/Ps52:2)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 21:8; 1 Samuel 22:9; 1 Samuel 22:18; 1 Samuel 22:22; Psalms 52:2


## דוב (id: 001587000000000)

דוב
===

דוב (H1727)

verb

Weak 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to cause to pine away \= causative action by which someone causes someone else's life to gradually lose its health and vitality

[LEV 26:16](https://ref.ly/Lev26:16)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 26:16

Relatives

kinsman, cousin exact meaning unsure; probably: \= close relative

[JER 32:12](https://ref.ly/Jer32:12)2 · [AMO 6:10](https://ref.ly/Amos6:10)3

1 SNG 5:1 RSV NIV NJB \[1a] \| NJPS NRSV REB GNT CEV \[1b] 2 JER 32:12 Usually translated as "uncle" \| but the immediate context suggests that this term refers to the son of one's uncle \| for this reason, a different meaning of the word has been proposed in this context: NJPS "kinsman" \| NRSV RSV NIV REB "cousin" \| CEV generalizes "he" \| GNT skips the word 3 AMO 6:10 NJPS gives a different interpretation, understanding מְסָרְפֹו as "who is to burn incense to him" (as part of burial rites)

Enio R. Mueller

mandrake, love apple \= wild perennial plant without stem; with large, fleshy, forked roots; with large oval leaves arranged in a rosette, purple flowers and yellow\-green fruits; ◄ mandragora officinarum; ► used medicinally as narcotic and purgative; ≈ because its roots resemble the lower part of the human body this plant was generally believed to induce conception; its fragrance was considered sweet

## דין (id: 001634000000000)

דין
===

דין (H1777b · A1778)

verb · דּוּן · דִּין · דַּיָּן · מָדֹון · מִדְיָן · מְדִינָה · אֲבִידָן

Judge 

|  |
| --- |

 Relief 

|  |
| --- |

 Safe 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ ישׁע · נחם · רִיב · שׁמר · שׁפט

to judge, to pass judgment, to vindicate, to rule \= action by which someone gives a verdict on a case or person in a dispute and ensures that the verdict is implemented, which, ideally, results in relief for the innocent and punishment for the guilty; this can only be done by someone in authority, such as a judge or ruler or even God himself

[GEN 15:14](https://ref.ly/Gen15:14) · [GEN 30:6](https://ref.ly/Gen30:6) · [GEN 49:16](https://ref.ly/Gen49:16) · [DEU 32:36](https://ref.ly/Deut32:36) · [1SA 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:10) · [EZR 7:25](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:25) · [JOB 36:31](https://ref.ly/Job36:31) · [PSA 7:9](https://ref.ly/Ps7:9) · [PSA 9:9](https://ref.ly/Ps9:9) · [PSA 50:4](https://ref.ly/Ps50:4) · [PSA 54:3](https://ref.ly/Ps54:3) · [PSA 72:2](https://ref.ly/Ps72:2) · [PSA 96:10](https://ref.ly/Ps96:10) · [PSA 110:6](https://ref.ly/Ps110:6)1 · [PSA 135:14](https://ref.ly/Ps135:14) · [PRO 31:9](https://ref.ly/Prov31:9) · [ISA 3:13](https://ref.ly/Isa3:13) · [JER 5:28](https://ref.ly/Jer5:28) · [JER 21:12](https://ref.ly/Jer21:12) · [JER 22:16](https://ref.ly/Jer22:16) · [JER 30:13](https://ref.ly/Jer30:13) · [ZEC 3:7](https://ref.ly/Zech3:7)

Conflict 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif

to dispute, to argue \= action by which humans engage in an argument with (other) humans or deities regarding a perceived injustice

[2SA 19:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam19:10) · [ECC 6:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl6:10)

## דלג (id: 001656000000000)

דלג
===

דלג (H1801)

verb

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 Leap 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ קפץ

to leap, to bound \= action by which animals move speedily by jumping over any obstacle that they find in their way; ≈ exclusively used metaphorically to refer to humans

[SNG 2:8](https://ref.ly/Song2:8) · [ISA 35:6](https://ref.ly/Isa35:6)

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to step over literally: to leap over something; hence: \= action by which humans put one leg in front of the other in order to move forward, with the specific intention to avoid touching an object that is located under one's feet

[ZEP 1:9](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:9)

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to scale literally: to leap (over a wall); hence: \= action by which humans climb over a high and steep object like a wall with relative ease as if they were leaping over an obstacle

[2SA 22:30](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:30) · [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30)

Enio R. Mueller

## דלל (id: 001665000000000)

דלל
===

דלל (H1809)

verb · דַּל · דַּלָּה

Low

to become low, to dwindle \= process by which the height of a body of water is diminished ◄ due to a drought

[ISA 19:6](https://ref.ly/Isa19:6)

Weak 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to grow weak \= process by which something's strength and ability to function is diminished

[ISA 38:14](https://ref.ly/Isa38:14)

Insignificant 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to be weak, to be helpless \= process by which an individual or group of people is reduced to a state of insignificance and becomes powerless to help oneself ◄ due to difficult circumstances such as poverty, sickness, and warfare

[JDG 6:6](https://ref.ly/Judg6:6) · [PSA 79:8](https://ref.ly/Ps79:8) · [PSA 116:6](https://ref.ly/Ps116:6) · [PSA 142:7](https://ref.ly/Ps142:7)

Lax 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to diminish, to dwindle \= process by which a prominent condition loses its prominence and becomes like its opposite

[ISA 17:4](https://ref.ly/Isa17:4)1

verb · דלה

Hang 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to hang, to dangle \= state in which something is suspended to an object in a way that it can swing freely

[JOB 28:4](https://ref.ly/Job28:4)2

1 ISA 17:4 NJPS interprets the word here as "dwindle", understanding כְּבֹוד in a physical sense as "mass". 2 JOB 28:4 There is much discussion over the meaning of דלל here. NJPS ("destitute of") understands it as having the same basic meaning of the other occurrences analysed in this entry. Most versions imply a root דלל II (cf. HALOT, DCH) meaning "to dangle".

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 19:6; Isaiah 38:14; Judges 6:6; Psalms 79:8; Psalms 116:6; Psalms 142:7; Isaiah 17:4; Job 28:4

## דָּם (id: 001673000000000)

דָּם
====

דָּם (H1818)

noun m

blood \= red liquid that circulates in the arteries and veins of humans and animals; ► used in rituals such as sacrifices, purification and covenant ceremonies, and never to be eaten; ≈ regarded as the seat of life; human blood, when flowing from the body, pollutes the body and the land

Liquids

People

blood \> person literally: blood; hence: \= living human being, ◄ defined by the blood flowing through their veins

[DEU 27:25](https://ref.ly/Deut27:25) · [1SA 19:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam19:5) · [PSA 94:21](https://ref.ly/Ps94:21)

Dead

blood \> bloodshed \= causative action by which humans kill other humans in a violent way, usually involving the shedding of blood, which brings guilt upon the people committing these acts

|  |
| --- |

Engage 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal sg

## דְּרֹור (id: 001716000000000)

דְּרֹור
=======

דְּרֹור (H1865 · H1866)

noun m

Flow

liquid \= process by which a liquid flows slowly, forming large drops

[EXO 30:23](https://ref.ly/Exod30:23)

noun m

Free

liberty, freedom, release \= state of being free from control and not in the power of someone else, which is not restricted to slavery and captivity only, but includes financial debts; it also applies to farm land that is free from being "enslaved" by the farmer and is allowed to lay fallow; it also applies to inalienable possessions, such as land, which is released to return to its rightful owner

[LEV 25:10](https://ref.ly/Lev25:10) · [ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1) · [JER 34:8](https://ref.ly/Jer34:8) · [JER 34:15](https://ref.ly/Jer34:15) · [JER 34:17](https://ref.ly/Jer34:17) · [JER 34:17](https://ref.ly/Jer34:17) · [EZK 46:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek46:17)

noun f

Birds

swallow, martin \= small bird with long slender wings and short legs; it flies at great speed for long periods on end, twisting and turning, usually in fairly large groups, catching insects in the air as they fly; it makes its nest under overhangs on rock faces, in caves, or in human structures, such as buildings and the underside of bridges; ◄ \|iHirundo daurica\|i\*, \|iHirundo obsolete\|i\*, \|iDelichon urbica\|i\*

[PSA 84:4](https://ref.ly/Ps84:4) · [PRO 26:2](https://ref.ly/Prov26:2)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 30:23; Leviticus 25:10; Isaiah 61:1; Jeremiah 34:8; Jeremiah 34:15; Jeremiah 34:17; Ezekiel 46:17; Psalms 84:4; Proverbs 26:2

## דרך (id: 001718000000000)

דרך
===

דרך (H1869)

verb · דֶּרֶךְ · מִדְרָךְ

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hif

to tread, to set foot (on something), to march, to move \= action by which humans or animals move forward by lifting and setting down each foot in turn

[NUM 24:17](https://ref.ly/Num24:17) · [DEU 1:36](https://ref.ly/Deut1:36) · [DEU 11:24](https://ref.ly/Deut11:24) · [DEU 11:25](https://ref.ly/Deut11:25) · [JOS 1:3](https://ref.ly/Josh1:3) · [JOS 14:9](https://ref.ly/Josh14:9) · [JDG 5:21](https://ref.ly/Judg5:21) · [JOB 22:15](https://ref.ly/Job22:15) · [JOB 28:8](https://ref.ly/Job28:8) · [ISA 11:15](https://ref.ly/Isa11:15) · [ISA 59:8](https://ref.ly/Isa59:8) · [MIC 5:4](https://ref.ly/Mic5:4) · [MIC 5:5](https://ref.ly/Mic5:5)

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to make (someone) tread, set foot \= action by which deities cause humans or animals to move forward by lifting and setting down each foot in turn

[PSA 107:7](https://ref.ly/Ps107:7) · [HAB 3:19](https://ref.ly/Hab3:19)

Know 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to guide, to teach \= causative action by which humans or deities give instructions to (other) humans with respect to a certain aspect of life, ◄ as if they take them by the hand and lead them along the way

[PSA 25:5](https://ref.ly/Ps25:5) · [PSA 25:9](https://ref.ly/Ps25:9) · [PSA 119:35](https://ref.ly/Ps119:35) · [PRO 4:11](https://ref.ly/Prov4:11) · [ISA 42:16](https://ref.ly/Isa42:16) · [ISA 48:17](https://ref.ly/Isa48:17)

Impact 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hif

to trample, to tread upon \= action by which someone move their feet with force on a surface or object, usually in a repetitive way ► which causes an effect on the surface or object whereupon it happens; ≈ associated with aggression and control

[DEU 33:29](https://ref.ly/Deut33:29) · [JDG 9:27](https://ref.ly/Judg9:27) · [JDG 20:43](https://ref.ly/Judg20:43) · [1SA 5:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:5) · [NEH 13:15](https://ref.ly/Neh13:15) · [JOB 9:8](https://ref.ly/Job9:8) · [JOB 24:11](https://ref.ly/Job24:11) · [PSA 91:13](https://ref.ly/Ps91:13) · [ISA 16:10](https://ref.ly/Isa16:10) · [ISA 16:10](https://ref.ly/Isa16:10) · [ISA 63:2](https://ref.ly/Isa63:2) · [ISA 63:3](https://ref.ly/Isa63:3) · [ISA 63:3](https://ref.ly/Isa63:3) · [JER 25:30](https://ref.ly/Jer25:30) · [JER 48:33](https://ref.ly/Jer48:33) · [JER 51:33](https://ref.ly/Jer51:33) · [LAM 1:15](https://ref.ly/Lam1:15) · [AMO 4:13](https://ref.ly/Amos4:13) · [AMO 9:13](https://ref.ly/Amos9:13) · [MIC 1:3](https://ref.ly/Mic1:3) · [MIC 6:15](https://ref.ly/Mic6:15) · [HAB 3:15](https://ref.ly/Hab3:15)

Shape 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hif

**Collocation:** דרך קֶשֶׁת

to bend a bow literally: to tread the bow; hence: \= causative action by which humans step on a bow and bend it in order to put the bowstring in place ► to make it ready for shooting

[PSA 7:13](https://ref.ly/Ps7:13) · [PSA 11:2](https://ref.ly/Ps11:2) · [PSA 37:14](https://ref.ly/Ps37:14) · [ISA 5:28](https://ref.ly/Isa5:28) · [ISA 21:15](https://ref.ly/Isa21:15) · [JER 9:2](https://ref.ly/Jer9:2) · [JER 51:3](https://ref.ly/Jer51:3) · [LAM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Lam2:4) · [LAM 3:12](https://ref.ly/Lam3:12) · [ZEC 9:13](https://ref.ly/Zech9:13)

Shape 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

**Collocation:** דרך חֵץ

to bend a bow literally: to bend the arrow, where 'arrow' is used metonymically to denote the entire bow; hence: \= causative action by which humans step on a bow and bend it in order to put the bowstring in place ► to make it ready for shooting

[PSA 58:8](https://ref.ly/Ps58:8) · [PSA 64:4](https://ref.ly/Ps64:4)

Soldiers 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal ptc.act

**Collocation:** דרך קֶשֶׁת

archer literally: bender of a bow; hence: \= soldier who shoots with bow and arrows

[1CH 5:18](https://ref.ly/1Chr5:18) · [1CH 8:40](https://ref.ly/1Chr8:40) · [2CH 14:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr14:7) · [JER 46:9](https://ref.ly/Jer46:9) · [JER 50:14](https://ref.ly/Jer50:14) · [JER 50:29](https://ref.ly/Jer50:29) · [JER 51:3](https://ref.ly/Jer51:3)

Enio R. Mueller  
 Ryan Sikes

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 24:17; Deuteronomy 1:36; Deuteronomy 11:24; Deuteronomy 11:25; Joshua 1:3; Joshua 14:9; Judges 5:21; Job 22:15; Job 28:8; Isaiah 11:15; Isaiah 59:8; Micah 5:4; Micah 5:5; Psalms 107:7; Habakkuk 3:19; Psalms 25:5; Psalms 25:9; Psalms 119:35; Proverbs 4:11; Isaiah 42:16; Isaiah 48:17; Deuteronomy 33:29; Judges 9:27; Judges 20:43; 1 Samuel 5:5; Nehemiah 13:15; Job 9:8; Job 24:11; Psalms 91:13; Isaiah 16:10; Isaiah 63:2; Isaiah 63:3; Jeremiah 25:30; Jeremiah 48:33; Jeremiah 51:33; Lamentations 1:15; Amos 4:13; Amos 9:13; Micah 1:3; Micah 6:15; Habakkuk 3:15; Psalms 7:13; Psalms 11:2; Psalms 37:14; Isaiah 5:28; Isaiah 21:15; Jeremiah 9:2; Jeremiah 51:3; Lamentations 2:4; Lamentations 3:12; Zechariah 9:13; Psalms 58:8; Psalms 64:4; 1 Chronicles 5:18; 1 Chronicles 8:40; 2 Chronicles 14:7; Jeremiah 46:9; Jeremiah 50:14; Jeremiah 50:29

## דַּרְכְּמֹון (id: 001720000000000)

דַּרְכְּמֹון
============

דַּרְכְּמֹון (H1871) — דַּרְכְּמֹנִים

noun m

Weight 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אֲדַרְכֹּון

daric, drachma \= gold coin, used in Persian empire

## דְּרַע (id: 001721000000000)

דְּרַע
======

דְּרַע (A1872) — דְּרָע

noun f

arm \= each of the two upper limbs of the body, including the shoulder and extending until the hand; ≈ directly associated with strength and power

## דְּתָבַר (id: 001732000000000)

דְּתָבַר
========

דְּתָבַר (A1884)

noun m

Officials 

|  |
| --- |

 Judge

judge \= a person whose responsibility it is to give a verdict on a case or person in a dispute and ensure that the verdict is implemented, which, ideally, results in vindication for the innocent and punishment for the guilty

[DAN 3:2](https://ref.ly/Dan3:2) · [DAN 3:3](https://ref.ly/Dan3:3)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Daniel 3:2; Daniel 3:3
